      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        沟通交流能力
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        还有寻找快乐和创造幸福的能力。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
      <br/>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
         3.
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         关于方向
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="text-align:left; color:rgb(51,51,51); line-height:30px; text-indent:2em; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Tahoma,Verdana,STHeiTi,simsun,sans-serif; font-size:14px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0.8em">
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
         1
        </span>
       </span>
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         、网络与通讯
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <br/>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        我们学院开的专业都是最火的，网络与通讯其实很多地方和嵌入式系统有结合点，比如路由器和交换机其实都是嵌入式系统，连到网络的嵌入式设备也越来越多，也正因如此，网络与通讯已经成为最热门的专业了。这个世界早晚会被一网打尽的，网内的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        机根本就算不上主流，随着可移动计算的嵌入式设备的大量使用，微软、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        GOOGLE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、雅虎等企业也都挤进了网络与通讯领域。网络与通讯我甚至觉得已经可以算是基础课的一部分了，当然，你并不需要学网络与通讯的全部课程，因为底层细节基本上不需要开发人员全部了解，但李素科老师的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        INTERNET
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        高级编程应该选，而且这门课也算到软件开发里了。学了那门课，保证受益匪浅，不过基础不好的学那个会比较吃力。现在网络比较火的有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        VOIP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        P2P
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        相关的一些东东，做到底层就会和嵌入式有联系了；现在网络上的多媒体相关应用也很火，因为未来网络要传大量多媒体信息；而且网络安全又是网络发展的头等大事，所以网络与通讯又可以和网络安全结合。关键在于选课时要注意各学科交叉，各位要想好自己将来要从事的大概行业，然后就要重点突破了。这个网和人间的情网很相似
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        你或我
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        男或女
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        都逃不过的。此（情）网恢恢
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        疏而不露
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        你准备好触网了吗
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ?
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        未来世界的所有软件几乎都要有联网功能，通过网络升级或者做些更新什么的，搞软件不懂网络肯定是不可思议的事情，所以网络与通讯的知识多少也要了解一些才行，但具体了解深度要看你们自己的需要了。网络已经和英语一样成为基础性东东了，我个人建议至少要看一看那部经典的小电影，就是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        TCP/IP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        打包的那部，把网络世界非常生动的描绘了一下，看了觉得特爽。再说一下张德昭老师和高培春老师吧，他们都是业界的名人，高老师是非常受人尊敬的，我一正在实习的朋友曾经和我说，当他去贝尔面试时，当面试考官得知他听过几门高老师的课时，脸上露出羡慕的表情。张老师属于大师级人物，可能我们这些刚入行的小生有时候不太理解她，她很多年前就是贝尔大牛，有些网络教科书上的技术就是在她带领下研究出来的，这是我们这种没入门的人无法想像的。所以她上课时我们会觉得有些难以领会，请大家要做好心理准备。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
         2
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         、电子服务
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <br/>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        我感觉主要是企业计算，主要是指企业信息系统
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ERP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        软件（企业资源规划）、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        CRM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        软件（客户关系管理）、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SCM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        软件（供应链管理，即物流软件）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        银行证券软件
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        财务软件
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        电子商务
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        /
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        政务（包括各种网站），数据仓库，数据挖掘，商务智能等企业信息管理系统。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这个领域对人才的需求显然永远是数量最大的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        因为这是计算机应用最多的领域
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        .
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        搞这方面的好处是
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
        (1)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        人才需求量极大
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        从事企业计算的公司在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IT
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        企业中占了大多数。除非在专业上一无特长
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        一般在这一领域总能找到工作。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        (2)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这方面的入门门槛相对较低（如果你的软件功底不是很深
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        可考虑这一领域）
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        (3)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这方面的大公司较多
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        大公司要赚大钱
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        所以多将精力花在企业计算业务上
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        .
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        如与我院同学目前实习的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IBM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BEA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等公司都属这一领域的公司。如果将来想到大公司找一份相对稳定的工作，从事这方面机会要大很多。但从事这一领域的缺点也是明显的
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        由于这方面的入门门槛相对较低，虽然这方面的人才需求量是最大的，但将来竞争对手会较多。你会发现，即使他原不是学
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IT
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        专业的人，也许他突击几个月后，做得照样像模像样。特别是当你年纪渐大后，你可能会发现，后面的年轻人可能很容易追上你的水平。如果你将来到国外去工作，你可能会发现从事这领域的人更多且高手如云。当然，若你在这一领域经过多年企业经验，达到较高境界（如能设计软件架构），则身价永远是高的。国内在这方面人才领域的主要问题是，有经验的高手太少，皮毛了解的人太多。从事电子服务，最重要的技能型技术知识是（
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        架构与程序设计（
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        2
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）大型数据库系统
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Oracle)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        3
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）基于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        UML
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的系统分析与设计。如果说还有什么重要的技能，还可将
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        XML
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        与
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Web Service
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        技术包含进来，若你在这几个领域掌握较好，则不愁找不到工作。其中尤其以
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        最为重要，目前
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        已成为企业计算软件开发的最主要平台。希望我院同学无论将来想从事何种方向，都应学一下
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        课程，至少可为将来找工作备一手关键功夫。包括想从事嵌入式或其它领域的同学，也是很有必要学一下
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的，毕竟
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是目前最重要的平台之一，即使你将来不想从事企业计算领域，了解一下
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        也是必要的，就像一门常识课程一样。其它与企业计算关系较密切的技能还包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ot Net
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        架构与程序设计、软件测试技术、软件配置管理，该领域较高层次的技能包括数据仓库技术、构件与中间件技术、设计模式等。像通信协议分析与网络程序设计，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Unix
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        统管理等也属有些关系的课程。希望各位一定要在某个领域有深入的掌握。只是跟着听课，即使学了再多课程也是没用处的，自己钻研下去才是最重要的。只一个
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        便是博大精深的，足够你啃下去的，钻研下去，你会发现你还要学的相关知识还有很多（包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        EJB
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        XML
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Web Service
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Design Pattern
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等）虽然从事企业计算的人才很多，但以下企业计算领域无论国内外都属稀缺人才
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）掌握大型
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ERP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系统，主要是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系统，包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP Basis(
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系统管理）或
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP ABAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （编程）或
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        功能模块实施（特别是财务模块
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        FI
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的实施）。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        顾问身价是最高的，而且非常难找。其它大型
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ERP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系统，掌握
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PeopleSoft
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Oracle FinacialJ.D.Edward
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Siebel
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等大型
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ERP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        软件系统的人也很值钱。这方面的人之所以身价奇高，主要是因为这些软件很专业，特别大，很难有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        D
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        版可学习，只有特大企业（如世界
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        500
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>

      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

        90%
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        软件系统的机会，建议毫不犹豫地抓住，那将捧上一辈的金饭碗。在国外，会
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的人特别值钱。物以稀为贵，这永远是颠扑不破的真理。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的价值不仅是因为他是一个
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ERP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>

       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        料采购和生产计划等）。一般
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        500
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        强公司绝不会像国内很多企业那样，用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

        从头设计企业的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ERP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IBM,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        由于他本科的财经背景
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>

       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IBM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        负责财经方面的咨询，这是一个很经典的案例哟，请传真师兄原谅我未经允许就引用
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>

       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>

        如果你在

       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
