      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        尤其是在欧美、日本、新加坡等国家，对
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SAP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IBM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        大型机）人才的需求是很大的。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        <br/>
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
         3
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         、关于嵌入式系统方向（集成电路方向也可参考）
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <br/>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        嵌入式系统无疑是当前最热门最有发展前途的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IT
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        应用领域之一。嵌入式系统用在一些特定专用设备上，通常这些设备的硬件资源（如处理器、存储器等）非常有限，并且对成本很敏感，有时对实时响应要求很高等。特别是随着消费家电的智能化，嵌入式更显重要。像我们平常常见到的手机、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、电子字典、可视电话、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        VCD/DVD/MP3 Player
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、数字相机（
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）、数字摄像机
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (DV)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        U-Disk
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、机顶盒
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (Set Top Box)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、高清电视
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (HDTV)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、游戏机、智能玩具、交换机、路由器、数控设备或仪表、汽车电子、家电控制系统、医疗仪器、航天航空设备等等都是典型的嵌入式系统。嵌入式将会是我们数字化生存的基础
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        一台
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        里其实就已经嵌入了
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        10
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        几个单片机
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        一辆高档轿车大约要用到六七十个单片机
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ;
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        嵌入式处理器无所不在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        无处不在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        全世界的年产量超过
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        100
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        亿片
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这是怎样惊人的数字呀
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        !
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        嵌入式系统是软硬结合的东西，搞嵌入式开发的人有两类。一类是学电子工程、通信工程等偏硬件专业出身的人，他们主要是搞硬件设计，有时要开发一些与硬件关系最密切的最底层软件，如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BootLoader
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Board Support Package(
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        像
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BIOS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        一样，往下驱动硬件，往上支持操作系统），最初级的硬件驱动程序等。他们的优势是对硬件原理非常清楚，不足是他们更擅长定义各种硬件接口，但对复杂软件系统往往力不从心（例如嵌入式操作系统原理和复杂应用软件等）。另一类是学软件、计算机专业出身的人，主要从事嵌入式操作系统和应用软件的开发。如果我们学软件的人对硬原理和接口有较好的掌握，我们完全也可写
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BSP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        和硬件驱动程序。嵌入式硬件设计完后，各种功能就全靠软件来实现了，嵌入式设备的增值很大程度上取决于嵌入式软件，这占了嵌入式系统的最主要工作（目前有很多公司将硬件设计包给了专门的硬件公司，稍复杂的硬件都交给台湾或国外公司设计，国内的硬件设计力量很弱，很多嵌入式公司自己只负责开发软件，因为公司都知道，嵌入式产品的差异很大程度在软件上，在软件方面是最有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        "
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        花头
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        "
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        可做的，所以我们搞软件的人完全不用担心我们在嵌入式市场上的用武之地，越是智能设备越是复杂系统，软件越起关键作用，而且这是目前的趋势。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         从事嵌入式软件开发的好处是
        </span>
       </span>
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
         :
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <br/>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）目前国内外这方面的人都很稀缺。一方面，是因为这一领域入门门槛较高，不仅要懂较底层软件（例如操作系统级、驱动程序级软件），对软件专业水平要求较高（嵌入式系统对软件设计的时间和空间效率要求较高），而且必须懂得硬件的工作原理，所以非专业
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IT
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        人员很难切入这一领域；另一方面，是因为这一领域较新，目前发展太快，很多软硬件技术出现时间不长或正在出现（如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        处理器、嵌入式操作系统、
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MPEG
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        技术、无线通信协议等），掌握这些新技术的人当然很找。嵌入式人才稀缺，身价自然就高，越有经验价格就越高。其实嵌入式人才稀少
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        根本原因可能是大多数人无条件接触
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这需要相应的嵌入式开发板和软件
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        另外需要有经验的人进行指导开发流程。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        2
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）与企业计算等应用软件不同，嵌入式领域人才的工作强度通常低一些（但收入不低）。搞企业应用软件的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IT
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        企业，这个用户的系统搞完了，又得去搞下一个用户的，而且每个用户的需求和完成时间都得按客户要求改变，往往疲于奔命，重复劳动。相比而言，搞嵌入式系统的公司，都有自己的产品计划，按自己的节奏行事。所开发的产品通常是通用的，不会因客户的不同而修改。一个产品型号开发完了，往往有较长一段空闲时间（或只是对软件进行一些小修补），有时间进行充电和休整。另外，从事嵌入式软件的每个人工作范围相对狭窄，所涉及的专业技术范围就是那些（
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        RTOS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MPEG
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        802.11
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等），时间长了这些东西会越搞越有经验，卖卖老本，几句指导也够让那些初入道者琢磨半年的。若搞应用软件，可能下一个客户要换成一个完全不同的软件开发平台，那就苦了。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        3
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        哪天若想创业，搞自已的产品，那么嵌入式是一个不错的主意，这可不像应用软件那样容易被盗版。我们这届有个同学自己有点此类小生意
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        具体做什么的没细问
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        他每月要进货几千片
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        8
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        位单片机
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        现在自己已经有车有房了。还有现在开发的饭馆用的点菜
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台，可无线连网和上网），据说销路不错，饭馆点点
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        让客户点菜，多显派头档次。这些
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的硬件设计一般都是请其它公司给订做（这叫
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        “
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        贴牌
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ”:OEM
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ），都是通用的硬件，我们只管设计软件就变成自己的产品了。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="text-align:left; color:rgb(51,51,51); line-height:30px; text-indent:2em; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Tahoma,Verdana,STHeiTi,simsun,sans-serif; font-size:14px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0.8em">
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         从事嵌入式软件开发的缺点是
        </span>
       </span>
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
         :
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="text-align:left; color:rgb(51,51,51); line-height:30px; text-indent:2em; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Tahoma,Verdana,STHeiTi,simsun,sans-serif; font-size:14px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0.8em">
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        入门起点较高，所用到的技术往往都有一定难度，若软硬件基础不好，特别是操作系统级软件功底不深，则可能不适于此行。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        2
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这方面的企业数量要远少于企业计算类企业。特别是从事嵌入式的小企业数量较多（小企业要搞自己的产品创业），知名大公司较少（搞嵌入式的大公司主要有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Intel
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Motorola
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        TI
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Philip
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Samsung
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Sony
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Futjtum
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Bell-Alcatel
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、意法半导体
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Microtek
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、研华、华为、中兴通信、上广电等制造类企业）。这些企业的习惯思维方式是到电子、通信等偏硬专业找人。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        3
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）有少数公司经常要硕士以上的人搞嵌入式，主要是基于嵌入式的难度。但大多数公司也并无此要求，只要有经验即可。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        同学们若学习嵌入式，显然应偏重于嵌入式软件，特别是嵌入式操作系统方面，应是我们的强项。对于搞嵌入式软件的人，最重要的技术显然是（实际上很多公司的招聘广告上就是这样写的）
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        掌握主流嵌入式微处理器的结构与原理
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        2
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        必须掌握一个嵌入式操作系统
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        3
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        必须熟悉嵌入式软件开发流程并至少做过一个嵌入式软件项目。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        在嵌入式软件方面最重要的课程包括
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        嵌入式微处理器结构与应用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这是一门嵌入式硬件基础课程，我们说过，嵌入式是软硬件结合的技术，搞嵌入式软件的人应对
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        处理器工作原理和接口技术有充分了解，包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的汇编指令系统。若不了解处理器原理，怎么能控制硬件工作，怎么能写出节省内存又运行高速的最优代码（嵌入式软件设计特别讲究时空效率），怎么能写出驱动程序（驱动程序都是与硬件打交道的）？很多公司招聘嵌入式软件人员时都要
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <br/>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        求熟悉
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        处理器，将来若同学到公司中从事嵌入式软件开发，公司都会给你一本该设备的硬件规格说明书
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (xxx Specification)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，你必须能看懂其中的内存分布和端口使用等最基本的说明（就像
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        x86
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        汇编一样），否则怎么设计软件。有些同学觉得嵌入式处理器课程较枯燥，这主要是硬件课程都较抽象的原因。还有同学对
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        汇编不感兴趣，以
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <br/>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        为嵌入式开发用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        C
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        语言就足够了。其实不应仅是将汇编语言当成一个程序设计语言，学汇编主要是为了掌握处理器工作原理的。一个不熟悉汇编语言的人，怎么能在该处理器写出最优的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        C
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        语言代码。在嵌入式开发的一些关键部分，有时还必须写汇编，如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Bootloader
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等（可能还包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BSP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）。特别是在对速度有极高要求的场合（如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DSP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        处理器的高速图像采集和图像解压缩），目前还会用到汇编写程序的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        尽管用到的机会相对
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        C
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        要小得多。当你在一个嵌入式公司工作时，在查看描述原理的手册时，可能很多都是用汇编描述的，这是因为很多硬件设计人员只会写或者喜欢用汇编描述，此时你就必须看懂汇编程序，否则软硬件人员可能就无法交流。很多嵌入式职位招聘时都要求熟悉汇编。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        [
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        小知识
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        目前嵌入式处理器常见的有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PowerPC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MIPS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Motorola 68K
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

        占据了绝对主流（有资料说手机中几乎
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>

       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>

       </span>

     </span>

     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的开发板，供最终用户使用或供教学实验。在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这个食物链上，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>

       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Intel
       </span>
      </span>

       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Samsung
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等公司是小鱼，而华恒等则是虾米，最终用户（我们这些要采购嵌入式开发板的）则是喂虾米的。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Intel
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        早期生产的是低端
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM(Strong ARM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，相当于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 7),
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        现在转向主要生产高端
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>

       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>

      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      </span>

       </span>

      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 9
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
