       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        较便宜，可跑
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        uclinux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （是一个不支持高
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <br/>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        级内存管理功能的嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系统）、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        uc/os II
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等实时操作系统，但因处理器不带内存管理单元
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MMU
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （无内存分页和地址映射机制，所以不能使用虚拟内存），所以不能跑
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Windows CE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，另外通用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        中的某些内存管理功能也不能用在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 7
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 9
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        大都是一个带
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MMU
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        功能的高端处理器，可跑
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        或通用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的大多数功能。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM7
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        和
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM9
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的区别是在与体系结构上，前者是冯
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ·
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        诺伊曼结构，后者是哈佛结构
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ——
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        指令和数据总线是分开的。以上是我的一点了解，可能有不对的地方。我们学院有十几套
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 7
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发系统（采用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Samsung S3C44b0x
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发板，主要用于嵌入式处理器结构、实时操作系统等课程实验用），
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 9
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的系统好象也已经到了（采用的芯片我不知道也没去问），还有以前的十几套
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MPC860
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发板（听说价格都很贵，很容易损坏），同学应爱护使用和珍惜这样的实验机会。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        (2)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        嵌入式操作系统类课程
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        除了
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的实时性稍差外，大多数嵌入式操作系统的实时性都很强
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        所以也可称为实时操作系统
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Real Time Operating System.
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        从事嵌入式的人至少须掌握一个嵌入式操作系统
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        当然掌握两个更好
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ),
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这在嵌入式的所有技术中是最为关键的了。目前最重要的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        RTOS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        主要包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        第一类、传统的经典
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        RTOS:
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        最主要的便是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        操作系统，以及其
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Tornado
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发平台。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        因出现稍早，实时性很强（据说可在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1ms
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        内响应外部事件请求），并且内核可极微（据说最小可
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        8K
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ），可靠性较高等，所以在北美，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        占据了嵌入式系统的多半疆山。特别是在通信设备等实时性要求较高的系统中，几乎非
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        莫属。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的很多概念和技术都和
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        很类似，主要是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        C
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        语言开发。像
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Bell-alcatel
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Lucent
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、华为等通信企业在开发产品时，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        用得很多。但
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        因价格很高，所以一些小公司或小产品中往往
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        用不起。目前很多公司都在往嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        转（听说华为目前正在这样转）。但无论如何，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        在一段长时间内仍是不可动摇的。与
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Vxworks
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        类似的稍有名的实时操作系统还有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        pSOS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        QNX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Nucleus
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        RTOS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        第二类、嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        操作系统
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的前途除作为服务器操作系统外，最成功的便是在嵌入式领域的应用，原因当然是免费、开源、支持软件多、呼拥者众，这样嵌入式产品成本会低。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        本身不是一个为嵌入式设计的操作系统，不是微内核的，并且实时性不强。目前应用在嵌入式领域的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系统主要有两类
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        一类是专为嵌入式设计的已被裁减过的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系统，最常用的是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        uClinux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （不带
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MMU
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        功能），目前占较大应用份额，可在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM7
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上跑；另一类是跑在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 9
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上的，一般是将
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux 2.4.18
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        内核移植在其上，可使用更多的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        功能（当然
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        uClinux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        更可跑在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM 9
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上）。很多人预测，嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        预计将占嵌入式操作系统的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        50%
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        以上份额，非常重要。缺点是熟悉
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的人太少，开发难度稍大。另外，目前我们能发现很多教材和很多大学都以
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ucOS/II
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        为教学用实时操作系统，这主要是由于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ucOS/II
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        较简单，且开源，非常适合入门者学习实时操作系统原理，但由于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ucOS/II
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        功能有限，实用用得较少。况且熟悉了
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发，不仅在嵌入式领域有用，对开发
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        应用软件，对加深操作系统的认识也有帮助，可谓一举多得。据我所知，目前
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Intel
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Philip
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        都在大搞
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM+LINUX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的嵌入式开发，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Fujitum
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        则是在自己的处理器上大搞
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发。目前在嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        领域，以下几个方面的人特别难找，一是能将
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        移植到某个新型号的开发版上；二是能写
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        驱动程序的人；三是熟悉
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        内核裁减和优化的人。不过
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        LINUX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        有一个硬伤，就是没有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WINDOWS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        那样的友好方便美观的交互界面，不然微软帝国早就守不住了。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         第三类、
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Windows CE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        嵌入式操作系统
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :Microsoft
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        也看准了嵌入式的巨大市场，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        永远是最厉害的，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        出来只有几年时间，但目前已占据了很大市场份额，特别是在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、手机、显示仪表等界面要求较高或者要求快速开发的场合，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        目前已很流行（据说有一家卖工控机的公司板子卖得太好，以至来不及为客户裁减
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        目前主要为
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        4.2
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        版（
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        .NET)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，开发平台主要为
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE Platform Builder
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，有时也用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        EVC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        环境开发一些较上层的应用，由于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发都是大家熟悉的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        VC++
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        环境，所以我院学过
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Windows
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        程序设计课程的同学都不会有多大难度，这也是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        容易被人们接受的原因，开发环境方便快速，微软的强大技术支持，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发难度远低于嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。对于急于完成，不想拿嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        冒险的开发场合，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是最合适了（找嵌入式
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的人可没那么好找的），毕竟公司不能像学生学习那样试试看，保证开发成功更重要。根据不同的侧重点
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        还有两个特殊版本，一个是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MS PocketPC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        操作系
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <br/>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        统专用于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上（掌上电脑），另一个是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MS SmartPhone
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        操作系统用于智能手机上（带
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        功能的手机），两者也都属于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台。在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        和手机市场上，除
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        外，著名的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PDA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        嵌入式操作系统还有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Palm OS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （因出现很早，很有名）、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Symbian
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等，但在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的强劲冲击下，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Palm
       </span>

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>

       </span>
      </span>

        、通信协议及编程技术
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这包括传统的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        TCP/IP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        协议和热门的无线通信协议。首先，大多数嵌入式设备都要连入局域网或
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Internet
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，所以首先应掌握
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        TCP/IP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        协议及其编程，这是需首要掌握的基本技术；其次，无线通信是目前的大趋势，所以掌握无线通信协议及编程也是是很重要的。无线通信协议包括无线局域网通信协议
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        802.11
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        系列，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Bluetooth
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，以及移动通信（如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        GPRS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        GSM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        CDMA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等）。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        C
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、网络与信息安全技术
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        如加密技术，数字证书
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        CA,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        以及各种网络安全设备
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        包括硬件防火墙
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        入侵检测
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IDS,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        还有防毒墙
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,IPS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        中国在这方面还是没有自己优势的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        我们陈院长好象正在往这方面发展
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        .
        <br/>
        D
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DSP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        技术
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Digital Signal Process
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        数字信号处理的意思，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DSP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        处理器通过硬件实现数字信号处理算法，如高速数据采集、压缩、解压缩、通信等。数字信号处理是电子、通信等硬件专业的课程，对于搞软件的人若能了解一下最好。目前
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DSP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        人才较缺。如果有信号与系统、数字信号处理等课程基础，对于学习
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MPEG
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        编解码原理会有很大帮助。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        4
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）嵌入式开发的相关硬件基础
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        对于软件工程专业的学生，从事嵌入式软件开发，像数字电路、计算机组成原理、嵌入式微处理器结构等硬件课程是较重要的。另外，汇编语言、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        C/C++
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、数据结构和算法、特别是操作系统等软件基础课也是十分重要的。我们的主要目地是能看懂硬件工作原理，但重点应是在嵌入式软件，特别操作系统级软件，那将是我们的优势。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        我们的研究生里有些是学电子、通信类专业过来的，有较好的模拟电路和单片机基础，学嵌入式非常合适。嵌入式本身就是从单片机发展过来的，只是单片机不带
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，而现在很多嵌入式应用越来越复杂，以至不得不引入嵌入式操作系统。另外，为追求更高速的信号处理速度，现在在一些速度要求较高的场合，有不少公司是将一些
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DSP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        算法，如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MPEG
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        压缩解压缩算法等用硬件来实现，这就涉及到
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        HDL
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        数字电路设计技术及其
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        FPGA/IP
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        核实现技术，这方面的人目前市场上也很缺。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        (5)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        题外话
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        另外，能写驱动程序的人目前是非常紧缺的（驱动程序也可归于嵌入式范畴），包括桌面
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Windows
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        中的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DDK
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        开发环境和
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        WDM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        驱动程序。公司每时每刻都要推出新产品，每一个新产品出来了，要能被操作系统所使用，是必须写驱动程序的。写驱动程序就必须掌握操作系统
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Windows
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        或
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的内部工作原理，还涉及到少量硬件知识，难度较大，所以这方面的人很难找。想成为高手的同学，也可从驱动程序方面获得突破。不
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <br/>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        过听做这方面的朋友说
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        做过以后，你会发现也并不是怎样难的。其实搞驱动程序的工作是很舒服的，搞完一个版本就会空一段时间，只有等公司新的芯片推出或新的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        出现后，才需要再去开发新一版驱动。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
      <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
