        <span style="color:#4455aa; margin:0px; padding:0px">
         www.myembed.com
        </span>
       </a>
       <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这是我们这届的几个嵌入式方向的同学做的网站
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上边有许多资料免费下载的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        .
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        GOOGLE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        网上能搜索太多的关于嵌入式系统的讨论了，介绍给大家一个
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
      <a href="http://www.embyte.com/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,94,172); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span style="color:#4455aa; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
         http://www.embyte.com
        </span>
       </span>
      </a>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        非常不错，有很多有经验者谈自己的体会
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        投入到其中的论坛中，你会切身感到嵌入式学习的
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <br/>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        热潮。要么走
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM+WinCE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，要么走
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM+LINUX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，要么
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ARM+VXWORKS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。每个搞嵌入式的人都可选一条路，条条大路通罗马
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        .
        <br/>
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
         4
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         、软件开发等其它方向
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <br/>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这是所有方向的基础学科，也是最好的方向，因为可以非常灵活的选择应用领域，学点嵌入式就可以去
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        做嵌入式系统的应用软件开发，学点网络与通讯就可以去做网络方面的研发，这也是我所说的方向其实要与具体应用结合。无论网络还是嵌入式都会与具体现实应用结合，除了纯硬件，否则核心都是软件开发。算法是北大非常有名的屈老师讲，她讲课的经验实在太丰富了，如果有兴趣可以考虑。陈向群老师在操
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        作系统界也是非常有名气的，她的操作系统高级内容丰富，认真学也会有相当的收获的。李素科老师的经典课程
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        INTERNET
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        高级编程我就不多说了。软件开发的课或多或少我们肯定会接触到的，各位心中一定要记得应用的方向，然后再去选课。各科交叉得其实非常紧，应用也需要许多交叉学科的知识，这时候要不断的调整二只眼睛，不论是望远镜还是显微镜。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        别的方向我其实就不太了解了，象管理与技术，我经验不够，又没学过管理，虽然想往管理方向走，但我觉得纯管理的应该不是我们的方向吧？但是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        IT
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        企业里的许多经理确实是没什么技术背景，我实习公司的经理就不是学理的，但这种人往往有复杂的背景，而且如果有了一个这样没技术背景的，公司里别的经理就一定要有技术背景的了，所以纯管理的只能去那些公司里多数是技术牛人当经理的地方，这是我的看法。我觉得现在二种经理都缺，但更缺的是有技术背景的，因为纯管理的各个学校都有很多研究生，选择余地很大，人家来软院应该是为了找懂技术的管理者吧？这是我的看法，不一定对，请大家指正。集成电路我也不是很懂，不过它与嵌入式系统的关系会多些，有许多嵌入式系统要用到各种
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ASIC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        FPGA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        还有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SOC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，集成电路也是非常急需的专业，上海某大学号称其集成电路专业工程硕士研究生毕业后如果年薪少于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        7
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        万还是几万，退学费，可见这行的前景有多好了。有条件懂硬件的同学可以考虑这个方向，但是好象真正的高手也不容易当的，只是我实在无法给出更多的建议了。网络安全不知道现在还算不算一个方向，这个涉及的领域也很多，比如一个硬件防火墙，要有嵌入式处理器做核心，要对网络有很深的了解，要有网络编程，扫描算法，甚至正则表达式、文法与自动机的理论都会用上，是个很大很复杂的领域。但是社会是真需要，特别是我们社会主义中国，对网络安全要求比别的国家更高，现在好多博士和教授都在转向研究网络安全，各位如果有这个志向也是很好的。微软现在找人一个是测试，一个就是网络安全方面，当然它比较狠，直接整个公司整个公司的收购，以至于全球几大网络安全厂商的股价一直在大跌。以前我们学院
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        VC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是由潘爱民讲的，后来听说微软给强行挖走了，去微软做网络安全方面的东东了。不过接替潘老师的王亚沙老师也是非常优秀的，他讲课我最服的是他讲得非常幽默风趣，让你睡意全无
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）当然，他讲得确实好啦！
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; color:rgb(0,0,0)">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         新增游戏方向介绍
        </span>
       </span>
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
         ,
        </span>
       </span>
       <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
         数字艺术的可参考
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <br/>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        将游戏软件人才称为数字媒体软件人才可能更好听些，包括游戏软件策划（最缺游戏策划的人）、游戏软件美术
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        设计、游戏软件程序设计等多方面的人才，对软件学院，游戏软件程序设计当然是最合适的了。游戏软件人才的确目前很缺，听说很多游戏软件公司苦于没新人才补充，特别是没有高手补充，不得不相互挖人才，以至将游戏软件人才身价越抬越高。网上说日本教育部刚刚批准成立了日本第一家专门培养四年制游戏软件
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        人才的本科大学。其实国内很多大学，特别是软件学院都有搞游戏软件人才的设想，但目前很少有做成的，主要原因是找不到能上游戏软件课的教师，听说有个学校只能花很大的价钱从
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Korea
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        找老师来上课，果真缺到此等地步？已有很多青少年沉湎于网游而颓废的实例，好在还不至于上升到制造精神鸦片的高度，所以开发游戏软件的人也不必每日惭悔（但开发儿童益智类游戏软件的人是不需惭悔的），如果想想这是为发展民族软件产业做贡献，那反倒是一件有意义的事情了。不过听一家游戏软件公司的老板讲，搞游戏软件开发是非常辛苦的。若想自己创业，搞搞游戏软件是不错的主意。现在网上网站或公司都在收购游戏软件（特别是手机游戏软件，因为手机游戏用户可选从网站上
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        download
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        到手机上，不像网游那么复杂），按
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        download
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        次数分成或一次性收购的都有。我们的同学在校期间是否也可发点小财？搞得好，说不定可卖到国外网站，直接挣
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        $$$
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        呢。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        大致游戏分成以下几类
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        PC
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        类游戏，包括单机和网游。这类游戏开发平台基本上都是基于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        VC++
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        和
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DitrectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （如
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectShow
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectDraw
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        D3D
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        资料可直接到
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        网站上查）。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        和
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OpenGL
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是两个主要的图形标准，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OpenGL
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        跨平台（
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Unix/Windows
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上都可跑），尽管很多搞研究的人对
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OpenGL
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        赞不绝口，将
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        骂得一文不值，但事实是，在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Windows
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台上，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是最快最方便的，所以在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Windows
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台上的游戏还是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        当家。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        2
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        手机游戏
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        目前手机游戏主要开发平台有两类
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        第一类手机游戏是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (Java 2 Micro Edition)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        本是为嵌入式平台设计的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Java
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，但由于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Java
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        生来就需要
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Java
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        虚拟机
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (JVM)
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        来解释，所以在嵌入式产品很少用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （太慢太耗内存）。但在手机游戏中
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        倒有用武之地，我想这可能主要是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Java
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        可跨
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台的原因，因为手机的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是千奇百怪的。我对
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        完全外行，但上次听
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Square Enix
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        公司的人说，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        与我们同学学过的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2EE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        还是有较大差别的。据我所知，目前手机中用的较多的是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        语言，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是运行在一种叫
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        K Java Virtual Machine
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的解释器上
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (K JVM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SUN
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        早期为演示
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        在嵌入式系统应用而开发的一个虚拟机
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        )
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，所以将在
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        K JVM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        上运行的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        叫
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。尽管
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        SUN
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        说今后不保证支持
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        K JVM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，将开发新的更高性能的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        虚拟机取而代之，但由于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        出现较早，很多早期的手机游戏软件都将
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        K JVM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        假想成
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        虚拟机的标准了，所以目前有大量的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        手机游戏软件存在，而且还在用
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        继续开发。特别是日本的手机游戏软件由于开发较早（像叫什么
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        docomi
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的日本最大的电信运营商手机游戏搞得很火），多是基于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的。所以目前市场上在招聘手机游戏软件人才时，很多要求掌握
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJava
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。有关
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        请到
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Sun
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的网站上找资料。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        另一类手机游戏是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BREW
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BREW
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        是美国高通公司
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        (Qualcomm
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        CDMA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        核心技术都是该公司开发的，有无数移动通信技术专利
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        )
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        发明的，据说可编译成二进制代码，那当然快了。主要的开发语言是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        C/C++
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。但迫于被指责为较封闭的压力，目前
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Qualcomm
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        已推出
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BREW
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台上的
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        虚拟机（但可想像那将是怎样慢的速度）。
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Qualcomm
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        搞定了很多手机制造商签定
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BREW
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        授权许可协议，最狠的是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Qualcomm
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        与中国联通绑在一起大堆基于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BREW
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的手机游戏，所以有些公司招聘时要求掌握
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        BREW
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        也就不奇怪了。将来谁会更火，我估计随着手机硬件资源的不断提高，不会在乎一个
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        JVM
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        的开销，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        J2ME
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        应更有前途，毕竟它是更开放的。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        3
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        专用游戏机
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        如电视游戏，
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        XBOX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等，我不太了解，不过这些游戏也太偏了。同学可看大宇资讯股份有限公司对网游和手机游戏的人才需求，很有代表性。从中我们可看出，游戏公司对人才的需求主要是以下技术
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        1
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        计算机图形学，特别是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        3D
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        编程与算法，包括
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        或
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OpenGL
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。开发平台是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        VC++/DIRECTX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        或
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        KJAVA
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        2
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        公司说，手机游戏因手机资源有限，必须对图像进行压缩，所以若有一些图像压缩算法知识比较好。像若能有
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MPEG
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        压缩算法较好，手机上采用的是比
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MPEG
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        压缩得更狠的一些特殊算法，但触类旁通。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        3
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        TCP/IP Socket
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        编程是搞网游开发的人必须掌握的。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        4
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        人工智能知识
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        复杂游戏可能需要一些
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        AI
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        算法。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        （
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        5
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ）
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        网络与信息安全知识
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        :
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        网游要防外挂。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        有些公司的网游服务器是基于
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        平台的，所以还提出了对游戏服务器端软件工程师的技术需求（精通
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MSSQL
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ORACLE
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        、
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        MYSQL
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        等数据库，精通
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Linux Programming
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        ，特别是
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        Socket
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        编程）。还有对维护游戏网站人才需求（
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ASP .NET
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        和数据库）。详细请同学自己看服务器。注意一条，最好有自己的游戏软件作品，若你应聘时能带一个
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        作品，那将有多强的竞争力，所以最重要的是现在就要行动，实践，实践，再实践。
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        关于游戏方向，目前，会
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>

       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        DirectX
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="color:#000000; margin:0px; padding:0px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

        <br/>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        昨晚李明曾经教过大家一个游戏，左右手的游戏，说明一件事情，那就是我们其实并不一定很了解自己。人生的这些选择应该要先了解自己，然后再去决定。许多人拼命打听别人选什么方向，选什么课程，别人和你是完全不同的，他们不知道你过去，不知道你的兴趣，和你完全不同的经历和背景，没有太多可比性。所以不如多花些时间想想自己到底喜欢什么样的生活，别人不能代替你，不管现在流行什么技术，不管哪个专业学好了都会很赚钱的，所以没必要去那么急功近利。路遥知马力，日久见人心，重要的是你做的决定是负责任的，是自己的决定就
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        OK
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        了，别的事情你把握不了。今天有了这样的理想，就去实践就去追求，也许路上发现错了，也可以改目标的，当然尽可能少改会比较省时间，但其实也无所谓了，人活着干任何事都不会白干的。你会在这里增长许多知识和见识，会认识许多大师级的人物，会有许多真心的朋友，会有难忘的回忆。身心健康，开心生活，有非常好的人际关系难道不比选什么课选什么方向更重要吗？别在匆忙的现实生活中迷失我们自己的兴趣，我希望你们不要随波逐流，希望你们每个人都活出真我的风采！好了，现在选什么，你们自己决定吧，重要的是你们已经来了软院这个大家庭，已经翻开了人生更美丽的一页，前面的路你只需要自信的走下去就好了。
       </span>

       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        这是一个成长的过程
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        不会因为我说哪个课好
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
        ,
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        就像爱的代价一样
       </span>

       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      </span>
      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        人终归要自己去亲身经历成长才行
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">

       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        然后就会成长
       </span>

       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">

        就会找到心中的梦
       </span>

      <span style="font-family:宋体; margin:0px; padding:0px">
       <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
        找到如何实现梦的方法
       </span>

      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:10.5pt">
       <span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; margin:0px; padding:0px">
